<h2 style='margin-left:0in;text-indent:0in'><span style='font-size:18.0pt;
line-height:103%'>Abstract</span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>The
consumption of fish and poultry products is rising along with the global
population. Increased housing and better management of chicken and fish are two
potential techniques to boost production to fulfil this need. However, such a
technique makes it very difficult for farmers to keep track of the production,
health, and welfare conditions of all their poultry and fish properly, in
addition to staffing issues. The project aims to create an Internet of Things
(IoT)-based smart poultry and fish farm system that can control and monitor
both poultry and fish farms simultaneously. In this project, automatic feeding
and monitoring of water level, room temperature, water ph., and turbidity using
the internet of things and a smartphone application called Blynk that will
allow for the simultaneous cultivation of fish and chicken.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:150%'><b><i><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>Keywords:</span></i></b><b><i><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>
Potential benefits, efficiency, Cost reduction, Automation, Revolutionizing</span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:150%'><b><i><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:150%'><b><i><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:150%'><b><i><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:150%'><b><i><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:150%'><b><i><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:150%'><b><i><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:150%'><b><i><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:150%'><b><i><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:150%'><b><i><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:150%'><b><i><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:150%'><b><i><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:150%'><b><i><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></i></b></p>

<h2 style='margin-left:21.3pt;text-indent:-21.3pt'><span style='font-size:18.0pt;
line-height:103%'>1.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:103%'>Introduction</span></h2>

<h3 style='margin-left:40.0pt;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%'><b><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black'>1.1<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'> </span></span></b><b><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black'> Background of Study and Motivation</span></b></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:42.55pt;text-align:justify;line-height:
150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>The
farming of fish and poultry is one of the largest industries in our country.
However, it is seriously concerning that Bangladeshis continue to engage in
conventional farming. Some students also want to start farming, but they need
longer opportunities&nbsp;to do so because they don't have vast
knowledge&nbsp;about conventional farming, or for other reasons. We will therefore
build a farming assistance system based on the Internet of Things using an
Arduino Uno. With this project, farming will require a great deal less time and
work. The goal of this project is to apply contemporary technologies in poultry
and fish farming to track and manage environmental variables that are crucial
to a farm's operations.</span><span style='font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>
</span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>Here,
we have categorized the issue under K5, K6, and K8 characteristics based on the
knowledge profile. Additionally, it fits into P1, P4, and P7 of the Complex
Engineering Problem Solving Characteristics</span></p>

<h3 style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%'><b><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black'>1.2<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'> </span></span></b><b><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black'> Project Objectives</span></b></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:.8pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
.5in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;
font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'> The main objectives of this project are:<b>
</b></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;
margin-bottom:.8pt;margin-left:56.7pt;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Symbol'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'>To automate the
watering and feeding of the fish and poultry farms.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;
margin-bottom:.8pt;margin-left:56.7pt;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Symbol'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'>To develop an
automated system that can simultaneously run several fish and poultry farms.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;
margin-bottom:.8pt;margin-left:56.7pt;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Symbol'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'>To monitor and
maintain a healthy environment for poultry birds and fish on the farm. </span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;
margin-bottom:.8pt;margin-left:56.7pt;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Symbol'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'>Temperature, ph. and
turbidity monitoring on an OLED display and control by app.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:.8pt;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<h3 style='margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%'><b><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>1.3<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'> </span></span></b><b><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'> A</span></b><b><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black'> brief outline of the report</span></b></h3>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:56.7pt;text-indent:-.25in;
line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'>Develop a
business plan that outlines the goals and objectives of the fish and poultry
farm.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:56.7pt;text-indent:-.25in;
line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'>The project's
planned operating model.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:56.7pt;text-indent:-.25in;
line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'>Components'
descriptions and implementation: using an OLED display, LEDs, a servo and water
motor, an ultrasonic sensor, a temperature, a pH sensor, a turbidity sensor, a
water level sensor, and a moisture sensor.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:56.7pt;text-indent:-.25in;
line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'>Establish a
Production Process: Create an effective, economical, and customer-satisfying
production process.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:56.7pt;text-indent:-.25in;
line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
Symbol'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'>Setup for the
experiment and numerical analysis.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:56.7pt;text-indent:-.25in;

</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'>Measured response
and research findings.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;

<h2 style='margin-left:21.3pt;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:18.0pt;
line-height:103%'>2.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:103%'>Literature Review</span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.3pt;text-align:justify;line-height:
150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>In
the agriculturally prosperous nation of Bangladesh, where fish and chicken meat
and eggs are vital sources of protein, vitamins, and minerals, new methods of
artificial control are being created daily. Rich natural excrement is produced
by chickens, which is also a significant source of income and employment for
many farmers and other people involved in related activities in the poultry
industry. In Bangladesh, chicken is the meat that is most widely recognized.
Because poultry meat is high in protein, low in calories, and low in
cholesterol, it is becoming increasingly popular in most nations. The authors
provide a low-cost Internet of Things-based remote poultry management system
that small- to medium-sized farmers can adopt. The authors use a range of
sensors that can measure and regulate temperature, humidity, water level, and
lighting. The authors' proposed study aims to help achieve some of the UNSDGs,
such as infrastructure improvement, business innovation, and the abolition of
hunger [1].</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.3pt;text-align:justify;line-height:
150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>The
author wants to develop an intelligent system for chicken farms. The
recommended system collects sensor data from the farm, such as moisture,
temperature, and humidity. After that, the developed method will automatically
manage and maintain the prevailing circumstances properly [2].</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.3pt;text-align:justify;line-height:
150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>This
article aims to describe how to build an automated Environment Controlled
Poultry Management System (ECPMS) utilizing readily available minimum
resources. The system has been rigorously studied for temperature, humidity,
air quality, and other physical characteristics essential for effectively
maintaining chickens. It was found that in addition to monitoring specific
features, the system also successfully modifies them. The framework was proven
to be very beneficial for farmers because they could access and control the
system remotely using their portable mobile devices [3]. The author of the
study discusses the use of intelligent sensing technologies in the poultry
industry to keep track of critical environmental factors necessary for chicken
production, such as air temperature, relative humidity, light, and air quality.
Regarding the measurement of these indicators and their effects on bird
welfare, the state of industry practice is currently addressed. As a result,
they looked into how intelligent sensing technology is used in the poultry
sector [4].</span></p>

<h2 style='margin-left:21.3pt;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:150%'>3.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:150%'>Methodology</span></h2>

<h3 style='margin-left:39.3pt;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%'><b><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black'>3.1<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'> </span></span></b><b><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black'> Introduction</span></b></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:6.95pt;
margin-left:42.55pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.5pt;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>The
chicken house, fish pond, smart feeder, automatic watering system, temperature
monitoring system, ph. monitor, and turbidity meter on an OLED display are the
main components of this project. The intelligent feeder is the first feature. A
sensor installed in the farm's door will detect any hens entering. The food
will start to flow if it sees the birds. Ten seconds will pass before the
sensor detects anything. A system for automatic irrigation is the second
feature. The motor will automatically turn on and begin pouring water for the
chicken once the water level falls below the desired level. The temperature
monitoring system is then displayed on an OLED screen. A temperature sensor
detects whenever the farm's temperature rises too high for the chickens,
turning on a red light and saying the temperature is Celsius. The green light
will turn on once the temperature is at an average level. The blink app also
controls automatic feeding for fish, and you can see the pH and turbidity
levels on display.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:6.95pt;
margin-left:-.25pt;text-indent:-.5pt;line-height:150%'><span style='font-family:
"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:6.95pt;
margin-left:-.25pt;text-indent:-.5pt;line-height:150%'><span style='font-family:
"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:6.85pt;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:6.85pt;line-height:150%'><b><u><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'><span
 style='text-decoration:none'>&nbsp;</span></span></u></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:6.85pt;line-height:150%'><b><u><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'><span
 style='text-decoration:none'>&nbsp;</span></span></u></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:6.85pt;line-height:150%'><b><u><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'><span

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:6.85pt;line-height:150%'><b><u><span

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:6.85pt;line-height:150%'><b><u><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'><span
 style='text-decoration:none'>&nbsp;</span></span></u></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:6.85pt;line-height:150%'><b><u><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'><span
 style='text-decoration:none'>&nbsp;</span></span></u></b></p>

<h3 style='margin-left:39.3pt;text-indent:-.25in'><b><span style='font-size:
14.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;color:black'>3.2<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'> </span></span></b><b><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black'> Working principle of the proposed project: </span></b></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;</p>

line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>                                    </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>Table:
1</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:39.3pt;text-indent:-.25in'><b><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;color:black'>3.3<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>
</span></span></b><b><span style='font-size:14.0pt'> Process of Work</span></b><b><span
style='font-size:14.0pt'>                                                                      
</span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:42.55pt;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>Here,
we'll be able to monitor and run farms digitally, and the fish and poultry will
develop in a controlled environment to boost output. We create systems that
automatically feed and check water levels, room temperature, water PH, and
turbidity. We used an ultrasonic sensor to provide the chickens and distribute
water automatically, and we used a water pump and a soil moisture sensor. A
soil moisture sensor is used to measure the water level in the container. When
the water level becomes too low, the soil moisture sensor instructs the pump to
start. When the water entered the container, the pump automatically stopped
using the temperature sensor LM35. When the temperature is hot or regular, two
lights show it. The red light will illuminate, and the cooling fan will turn on
if the temperature is high. The temperature is indicated by a green light when
it is normal. We work to develop automatic fish feeding with servo motors that
the Blynk app can manage. We also utilize a turbidity sensor and a ph sensor to
determine the turbidity of the water. The Blynk app can monitor and manage all
of these systems.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:42.55pt;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<h3 style='margin-left:39.3pt;text-indent:-.25in'><b><span style='font-size:
14.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;color:black'>3.4<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'> </span></span></b><b><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black'> Description of the components</span></b></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:.8pt;
margin-left:-.25pt;text-indent:-.5pt;line-height:150%'><b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:#4472C4'>         </span></b></p>

<h4 style='margin-left:78.0pt;text-indent:-.5in'><b><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;color:black;
font-style:normal'>3.4.1<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:
"Times New Roman",serif;color:black;font-style:normal'>Arduino UNO R3</span></b></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:78.0pt;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>Arduino UNO is a
microcontroller board based on the ATmega328P.It contains everything needed to
support the microcontroller; connect it to a computer with a USB cable or power
it with an AC-to-DC adapter or battery to get started. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:78.0pt;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>Memory:       1. AVR CPU
at up to 16 MHz </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:78.0pt;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>                       2.
32KB Flash </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:78.0pt;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>                      
3.2KB SRAM </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:78.0pt;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>                      
4.1KB EEPROM </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:78.0pt;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>Power:            2.7-5.5
volts       </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:78.0pt;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>                               
</span></p>

<div align=center>

<table class=MsoTableGrid border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none'>
 <tr>
  <td width=361 valign=top style='width:271.0pt;border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  0in;margin-left:0in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'><img
  width=348 height=177 id="Picture 1598"
  src="Report-of-project-micro_files/image002.jpg"></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;
margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:0in;text-align:center;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>Fig
1: Arduino UNO</span></p>

<h4 style='margin-left:78.0pt;text-indent:-35.45pt'><b><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;color:black;
font-style:normal'>3.4.2<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:
"Times New Roman",serif;color:black;font-style:normal'>Soil moisture sensor</span></b></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:78.0pt;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>The
soil moisture sensor consists of two probes used to measure water's volumetric
content. The two probes allow the current to pass through the soil, and then it
gets the resistance value to measure the moisture value.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;
margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:78.0pt;text-align:center;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'><img width=303 height=182
id="Picture 1674" src="Report-of-project-micro_files/image003.jpg"></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;
margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:0in;text-align:center;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>              
Fig 2: Soil moisture sensor</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;
margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:0in;text-align:center;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:4.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<h4 style='margin-left:78.0pt;text-indent:-.5in'><b><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;color:black;
font-style:normal'>3.4.3<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:
"Times New Roman",serif;color:black;font-style:normal'>Ultrasonic module
HC-SR04</span></b></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:78.0pt;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>Ultrasonic
ranging module HC-SR04 provides a 2cm – 400cm non-contact measurement function,
and the ranging accuracy can reach 3mm. It uses Ian O trigger for at least 10us
high-level signal. The Module automatically sends eight 40 kHz and detects
whether there is a pulse signal back.   </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='margin-top:10.0pt;text-align:center;
line-height:150%'><span style='font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'><img
width=231 height=180 id="Picture 1676"
src="Report-of-project-micro_files/image004.jpg"></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;

style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>Fig
3: Ultrasonic module HC-SR04</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:0in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'> </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:

</span></span></b><b><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:

style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>The
LM35 device is rated to operate over a −55°C to 150°C temperature range, while
the LM35C device is rated for a −40°C to 110°C degree. Operates From 4 V to 30
V. 0.5°C Ensured Accuracy (at 25°C).</span></p>

<h4 style='margin-left:78.0pt;text-indent:-.5in'><b><span style='font-size:

font-style:normal'>3.4.10<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:
"Times New Roman",serif;color:black;font-style:normal'>Ph sensor</span></b></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:78.0pt;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>A
number between 0 and 14 represents the normal pH range. The chemical is
described as balanced when its pH value is 7. Higher alkalinity is indicated by
pH values above 7, whilst more acidic compounds are those with pH values below
7.<img width=342 height=165 id="Picture 3"
src="Report-of-project-micro_files/image011.jpg"></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;
margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:0in;text-align:center;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>Fig
10: Ph sensor</span></p>

<h4 style='margin-left:78.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.5in;line-height:
150%'><b><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black;font-style:normal'>3.4.11<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
"Times New Roman",serif;color:black;font-style:normal'>Breadboard</span></b></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;
margin-left:78.0pt;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>The purpose of the
breadboard is to make quick electrical connections between components- like
resistors, LEDs, capacitors, Etc. so that user can test their circuit before
permanently soldering it together. Height / Thickness: 0.5118 inch. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;
margin-left:78.0pt;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>Length: 7.87 to 47.24 inch. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;
margin-left:78.0pt;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>Units: Metric. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;
margin-left:78.0pt;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>Width: 7.87 to 47.24 inch  </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;
margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:0in;text-align:center;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'><img width=392 height=185
id="Picture 1949" src="Report-of-project-micro_files/image012.jpg"></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;

11: Breadboard</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>Table:
3</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:6.85pt;
margin-left:-.25pt;text-indent:-.5pt;line-height:150%'><b><u><span
style='font-size:15.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'><span
 style='text-decoration:none'>&nbsp;</span></span></u></b></p>

<h2 style='margin-left:21.3pt;text-indent:-.25in'><span style='font-size:18.0pt;
line-height:103%'>7.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:103%'>Experimental results</span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:35.35pt;margin-bottom:
7.15pt;margin-left:21.3pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.5pt;line-height:
150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>The
ultrasonic sensor should be no closer than 10 cm when the chicken enters; if it
is, the sensor will detect the fowl, and the intelligent feeder will begin to
flow automatically. The lights are temperature-dependent; if the temperature is
above 29 °C, the heating light (red light) will automatically turn on and
appear on display; if the temperature is below 30 °C, the usual green light
will turn on. The user can alter this threshold value.</span></p>

<h4 style='margin-left:39.3pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in'><b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black;font-style:normal'>7.1<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:
"Times New Roman",serif;color:black;font-style:normal'>The Summary of
Experimental value of the temperature and lights for poultry </span></b></h4>

<h4 style='margin-left:39.3pt;text-align:justify'><b><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;color:black;
font-style:normal'>birds</span></b></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;</p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'>Table 4</p>

<h4 style='margin-left:39.3pt;text-indent:-.25in'><b><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;color:black;
font-style:normal'>7.2<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></b><b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black;font-style:normal'>The Summary of Experimental value of the chicken
distance from the sensor and smart feeder status for poultry birds</span></b></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:4.0pt;line-height:107%'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<table class=TableGrid border=0 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 width=529
 style='width:396.9pt;margin-left:35.2pt;border-collapse:collapse'>
 <tr style='height:49.9pt'>
  <td width=76 style='width:56.7pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;padding:8.75pt 5.75pt .3pt 5.3pt;
  height:49.9pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal align=center style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;
  margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.1pt;text-align:center;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>Week</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black'>Table 8</span></p>

<h3 style='margin-left:39.3pt;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%'><b><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black'>8.2<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'> </span></span></b><b><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black'> Ultrasonic</span></b><b><span style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:
150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;color:black'> sensor</span></b></h3>

<h4 style='margin-left:78.0pt;text-indent:-.5in'><b><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;color:black;
font-style:normal'>8.2.1<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:
"Times New Roman",serif;color:black;font-style:normal'>Comparison between
numerical and experimental results of Ultrasonic sensor</span></b></h4>

<table class=TableGrid border=0 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 width=510
 style='width:382.7pt;margin-left:77.75pt;border-collapse:collapse'>
 <tr style='height:26.75pt'>
  <td width=170 style='width:127.55pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;padding:8.75pt 5.75pt .3pt 5.3pt;
  height:26.75pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal align=center style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;
  margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:.1pt;text-align:center;line-height:150%'><span

<h3 style='margin-left:39.3pt;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%'><b><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black'>8.3<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'> </span></span></b><b><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black'> pH sensor</span></b></h3>

<h4 style='margin-left:78.0pt;text-indent:-.5in;line-height:150%'><b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black;font-style:normal'>8.3.1<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></b><b><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
"Times New Roman",serif;color:black;font-style:normal'>Comparison between
numerical and experimental results of pH sensor</span></b></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;
margin-left:.5in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:4.0pt;line-height:
150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

  <td width=76 rowspan=3 style='width:56.7pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;padding:8.75pt 5.75pt .3pt 5.3pt;height:21.35pt'>

  margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:.1pt;text-align:center;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;color:black'>5</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=217 style='width:163.05pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;padding:8.75pt 5.75pt .3pt 5.3pt;
  height:21.35pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal align=center style='margin-bottom:8.0pt;text-align:center;
  line-height:150%'><span style='font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
  color:black'>NTU&lt;30</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=203 style='width:152.45pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;padding:8.75pt 5.75pt .3pt 5.3pt;
  height:21.35pt'>

  margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:.1pt;text-align:center;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;color:black'>NTU=30</span></p>
  </td>

  <td width=217 style='width:163.05pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;

</table>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:150%'><b><span
style='font-size:4.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black'>Table 11</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:49.65pt;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>We
obtained the greatest floating value in the experimental data, according to a
comparison between the numerical and experimental results. Regarding measuring
temperatures, there are modest differences between the numerical and
experimental data. If we look at week 5 of the experimental results, we can
observe that the temperature stays normal, however in the numerical analysis,
the temperature fluctuates between normal and heated. Only when the requirement
is met in both the numerical and experimental findings does the smart feeder
open.</span><span style='font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'> </span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>We
utilize pH sensors in the fish ponds to monitor and maintain the right pH for
the fish. We are aware that pond water pH should be as similar as possible to
fish blood for optimal results (i.e., 7.0 to 8.0). If the pH of the water falls
below 5 (due to acidic runoff, for example) or goes over 10 fish could become
stressed and perish (e.g., alkaline runoff). So, we simultaneously check and
regulate the pH level of our pond. It displays an average value between 6 and
8, which is suitable for a fish pond. A turbidity sensor was also present,
which can measure the clarity of pond water. The value is displayed in NTU.
Nephelometric Turbidity Unit is the abbreviation. The pond has a typical NTU of
30.</span><span style='font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'> </span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>A
value was obtained between 28 and 45 NTU. Our water pump automatically starts
filtering the water and maintaining water clarity once the NTU value exceeds
the standard</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:49.65pt;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:49.65pt;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:49.65pt;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:49.65pt;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:49.65pt;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:49.65pt;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:49.65pt;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<h2 style='margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-21.25pt'><span style='font-size:
18.0pt;line-height:103%'>9.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:103%'>Limitations of
the project </span></h2>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;
margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:49.65pt;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Symbol'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'>Manual setups,
which are necessary for Controlling sheds and call for expert labor,</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;
margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:49.65pt;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Symbol'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'>Another concern
to take into account with chicken production is the usage of antibiotics.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;
margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:49.65pt;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Symbol'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'>Some
environmental circumstances do not favor some birds &amp; fish.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;
margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:49.65pt;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Symbol'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'>Poultry illness
has the potential to cause the loss of an entire batch of chicks.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;
margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:49.65pt;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Symbol'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'>some faulty
sensors (Turbidity and pH sensor) and we faced some technical errors for that
problem.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:0in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:0in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:0in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:0in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:0in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:0in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<h2 style='margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt'><span style='font-size:
18.0pt;line-height:103%'>10.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-size:18.0pt;line-height:103%'>Conclusion and
future
endeavors                                                                  </span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:28.35pt;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>IoT-based
systems A revolutionary initiative called Smart Poultry and Fish Farm has the
potential to transform the poultry industry. Many businesses may provide
farmers with a profitable and inexpensive way to manage their poultry business
by leveraging technology. Investors and industry experts will be interested in
the farm's novel approach to poultry farming, and the farm will be in a good
position to take the lead in the sector.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:28.35pt;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>Smart
Poultry and Fish Farm will keep improving its technology and growing its
offerings in the future. The accurate recognition of chicken noises can be
utilized to analyze and anticipate information about fish and chicken diseases,
behavior, weight, age, happiness, and well-being through the application of
sound recognition technology and reliable algorithms. It is possible to utilize
IoT to investigate how vocalization affects chickens' levels of stress. It is
possible to hear when chickens are plucking their feathers by listening to
their sounds. As a result, the animal may suffer harm or perhaps perish. Fish
are the same way. The farm intends to provide new goods and services that will
aid farmers in boosting their output and profits. The farm will also be looking
into new markets and collaborations that would help it reach more consumers.
The smart Poultry Farm will undoubtedly grow to be a significant player in the
poultry business thanks to its creative approach and dedication to customer
care.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:0in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:0in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:0in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:0in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:0in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
0in;margin-left:0in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
150%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>
